 • Tap a task to start timing; tap it again to stop timing
 • Use the context menu for a task to list times
 • Change configuration options with the menu
 • View a weekly report with the menu
 
 Tapping a different task switches timing to the other task.
 
 The task context menu allows you to edit tasks (change their names), delete tasks (including all of the time history for that task!), or view the time log for that task.
 
 Time Log view
 
 The time log for a task is filtered on the same range that you selected for the main task view, so if you filtered the task view for This Week and you open the time log, then you'll only see times for this week. Use the Add Time menu item to manually insert times into the time log. Use the context menu for a time to delete or edit a time range.
 
 Note that TimeTracker will not prevent you from creating times that overlap with times in other (or the same) task. , x=82, y=303, h=1298, w=916, dsc=], txt=, exp=, tr=null] weight=1.0 ds=CS sc=com.markuspage.android.atimetracker.Bottom_Up.Expected..1.com.markuspage.android.atimetracker_0.20_9_augmented.png ex=0
